GT Equivalence Verification (PO9)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - mu*(c0 - x**c1)*v - omega0**c2*(gamma*Abs(v)**c3 + c4)*x - omega0**c5*x
Candidate formulas: 50

Let’s rewrite the GT in a clearer expanded form.

### Ground Truth (GT)
\[
\text{GT}(x,t,v)=0.3064552763\sin t\;-\;0.4243105872\,v(1-x^2)\;-\;1.9272891093\,x\big(0.06821634757|v|^{1/3}+1\big)\;-\;1.9272891093\,x
\]

Expand the \(v\) term:
\[
-0.4243\,v(1-x^2)= -0.4243\,v + 0.4243\,v x^2
\]

Expand the \(x(\cdots)\) term:
\[
-1.9273\,x(0.0682163|v|^{1/3}+1)= - (1.9273\cdot 0.0682163)\,x|v|^{1/3} -1.9273\,x
\]
and there is another \(-1.9273x\), so total linear-in-\(x\) is \(-3.8546x\).

So GT has these essential structures:
- a pure sinusoid in \(t\): \(A\sin t\)
- a linear \(v\) term: \(\alpha v\)
- a \(v x^2\) term: \(\beta v x^2\)
- a linear \(x\) term: \(\delta x\)
- a mixed non-polynomial term: \(x|v|^{1/3}\)

That last term \(x|v|^{1/3}\) is the key: none of the candidates include \(|v|^{1/3}\) (or any fractional power of \(|v|\)) multiplied by \(x\). Conditional domains like \(v\ge 0\) can turn \(|v|^{1/3}\) into \(v^{1/3}\), but you still need a fractional power term present in the candidate.

Now check candidates.

---

- Can match \(-0.4243v + 0.4243vx^2\) by choosing \(c5=-0.4243\), \(c2=0.4243\).

**No match.**

---

### Core obstruction (why none can match even with domain conditions)
GT contains the mixed fractional-power term \(x|v|^{1/3}\). None of the candidates contain any \(|v|^{p}\) with \(p=1/3\) (or any fractional power), so no choice of constants can create that dependence. Domain restrictions like \(v\ge 0\) only remove the absolute value, they do not create a fractional exponent where none exists.

Additionally, many candidates only allow time dependence multiplied by \(x\) or hidden inside exponentials, whereas GT has an additive standalone \(\sin t\) term.

Final verdict:
[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match

GT Equivalence Verification (PO9)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - mu*(c0 - x**c1)*v - omega0**c2*(gamma*Abs(v)**c3 + c4)*x - omega0**c5*x
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to analyze each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.424310587218182*v*(1 - x**2) - 1.92728910930903*x*(0.0682163475684738*Abs(v)**0.333333333333333 + 1) - 1.92728910930903*x + 0.30645527626767*sin(t)`

Let me expand this:
- `-0.424310587218182*v + 0.424310587218182*v*x**2`
- `-1.92728910930903*x*0.0682163475684738*Abs(v)**0.333333333333333 - 1.92728910930903*x`
- `-1.92728910930903*x`
- `+0.30645527626767*sin(t)`

Combining:
- `v` term: `-0.424310587218182*v`
- `v*x²` term: `+0.424310587218182*v*x²`
- `x*|v|^(1/3)` term: `-0.131504...*x*Abs(v)**(1/3)`
- `x` terms: `-1.92728910930903*x - 1.92728910930903*x = -3.85457821861806*x`
- `sin(t)` term: `+0.30645527626767*sin(t)`

So GT = `A*v + B*v*x² + C*x*|v|^(1/3) + D*x + E*sin(t)`

Key basis functions: `v`, `v*x²`, `x*|v|^(1/3)`, `x`, `sin(t)`

The critical distinguishing feature is `x*|v|^(1/3)` - this is a cube root of absolute value of v times x. This is NOT equivalent to `v*|v|`, `v³`, `v/(c+|v|)`, or polynomial terms in v.

Let me check each candidate for the presence of `|v|^(1/3)` or something that could produce it:

**None of the candidates contain `|v|^(1/3)` or `Abs(v)**(1/3)`.**

The candidates use approximations like:
- `v*|v|` (quadratic in v with sign)
- `v³` (cubic in v)
- `v/(c+|v|)` (rational in v)
- Pure `v` terms
- `exp` terms

None of these can exactly reproduce `|v|^(1/3)` since it's a fundamentally different basis function. By the linear independence principle, `|v|^(1/3)` cannot be expressed as any combination of `v`, `v³`, `v*|v|`, `v/(c+|v|)`, polynomials, exponentials, or trigonometric functions.

Let me verify this is truly required and non-zero: The coefficient is `-0.1315...` which is non-zero, so this term cannot be eliminated.

Therefore, **no candidate can match the GT**.

Let me do a quick sanity check on a few promising candidates like 35 and 37 that have `v*x²` and `v` and `x` terms plus `sin(t)`:

**Candidate 35:** `c0*x³ + c1*x² + c2*v*x² + c3*x + c4 + c5*v + c6*x*sin(c7*t + c8)` - Has `v`, `v*x²`, `x`, `x*sin(t)` but missing `x*|v|^(1/3)`. Extra `x³`, `x²` terms can be zeroed. But cannot produce `x*|v|^(1/3)`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 37:** Has `v*|v|` instead of `|v|^(1/3)`. **NO MATCH**

All candidates: NO MATCH due to missing `x*|v|^(1/3)` basis function.
